bsgrub bya 'di'i tshig stod cha sgra zhes pa der rgol phyi rgol gnyis kas khas lbangs kyang tshig smad cha 'jig pa de grangs can pas khas ma blangs stabs khyad  par rab tu grags pa ma yin pa'i skyon gyur to /
... khyad par la gnas pa'i don gzhan bkod pa /
don gzhan bkod pa'i rgyan gyi nang tshan zhig ste /
bsgrub bya brjod 'dod kyi dngos po byed las khyad par can zhig de'i sgrub byed du gang dang chos mtshungs pa'i byed las khyad par dang ldan pa zhig bkod pa'i rgyan /
... khyad 'phags /

phul byung gi rgyan gyi nang tshan zhig ste /

bsdus brjod kyi rgyan gyi nang tshan zhig ste /
dpe'i khyad gzhi dang khyad chos kyi gnas lugs brjod pa des /

mig dbang la rab rib nad byung ba'i dbang gis skra shad 'dzag par snang ba'i dbang shes lta bu /
yul la yod pa /
mgal me myur du bskor ba'i dbang gis 'khro lor snang ba'i shes pa lta bu /
de ma thag rkyen la yod pa /
zhe sdang drag pos yid shes 'khrul ba'i blo lta bu'o /
... 'khrul snang /
don dngos dang mi mthun pa'i nyams snang /
...  ma yin yin par 'char ba'i 'khrul snang /
...'khrul snang bden 'dzin /
...'khrul snang zang zing /
... 'khrul ba /
. tha mi dad pa nor ba'am 'dzol ba /
...sems 'khrul te skad cha gang byung bshad pa /
...don ma 'khrul bar gyis shig ... snang ba 'khrul ba /
...blo 'khrul nas mi dran pa /
... . rang gi snang yul la 'khrul ba'i rig pa /
dper na /
dung ser snang dang /
rtog pa'i snang yul lta bu med pa la yod pa dang min pa la yin par snang ba'o /
...rig pa bsgrims nas 'khrul ba zlog pa /
...'khrul ba rim gyis nyung du phyin pa /
...ming gi rnam grangs la nor ba dang /
'phyugs pa /
'dzol ba /
log shes bcas so /
'khrul ba mi mnga' ba /
sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi nang gses shig ste /
nyan thos la sogs pa ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi sgo nas las su byed pa la 'khrul ba 'byung gi /
sangs rgyas la de lta bu mi mnga' bas so /
... 'khrul bral lo 'pho /
skyon bton lo 'pho dang don gcig 'khrul zhig pa /
'khrul snang ma lus zhig pa'am yal ba ste stong nyid rtogs pa'i gang zag ... 'khrul gzhi /
nor 'khrul byung ba'i rgyu rkyen /
... 'khrul shes /
'du shes 'khrul ba'i sems te /
don dngos dang mi mthun pa'i mthong tshul dang bsam tshul /
... 'khrul so /
'khrul sa'am 'khrul ba'i rgyu rkyen /
... ltar snang 'khrul ba /
... 'khrus pa /
. 'khru ba'i 'das pa /
. rnying brtson pa /
... 'khren cha /
lha srung sogs kyis sems 'phreng ba'i 'khu ldog byed pa'i mtshan ma /
... 'khren pa /
rnying zhen pa'am chags pa /
...chags pa'i yul la 'khren pa /
...pha ma la sems 'khren pa /
...zas la 'khren pa /
... 'khreb to /
sems rengs po ste sems bcos dka' ba /
... 'khreb pa /
tha mi dad pa 'khrebs pa /
'khreb pa / /
sems rgyud rengs pa /
...rta rgod ma btul bas 'khreb pa /
... 'khrebs pa /
'khreb pa'i 'das pa /
'khrog pa /
tha mi dad pa 'khrogs pa /
'khrog pa / /
tshigs 'chus pa /
...rgan mo pus tshigs 'khrogs kyang 'gro snying 'dod /
... khog nang nas skad sgrog pa /
...grang bas khog pa 'khrog pa /
...grod pa sbos te 'khrogs pa /
... 'on pa /
...a mchog 'khrog tsam zhig  'dug ... 'khrogs pa /
'khrog pa'i 'das pa /
'khrobs /
'khrab pa'i skul tshig 'khrol 'khyil /
dngos po lhag lus /
... 'khrol cha /
dngos po'i lhag lus /
... dgongs pa ster ba'am gnang ba khrol ba /
...rang yul gnyen 'phrad du phyin chog pa'i 'khrol cha gnang ba /
... 'khrol po /
kha gsang po'am rnam 'gyur 'jam po ste sgam po min pa /
... gleng gtam 'khrol po 'dug ...kha gshis 'khrol po /
... 'khrol ba /
tha mi dad pa grol ba /
